A good novel doesn't always have to have perfect characters. If you want perfect and likeable characters that much, you should read \"The Notebook\". Yes, Ng·∫°n sounds like a loser, H√† Lan must be a utilitarian girl, D≈©ng is an f-boy. But that's why this story could have touched so many people- because it's realistic and it's relatable. Ng·∫°n, as I said- is just a below-average guy, but his loyal with Ha Lan is a symbol for a type of love that so many people on earth have experienced: the innocent, no self-interest emotions toward your crush, your first love. Sometimes this type of love is harmful to both of the parties, but it's love regardless and that's why Ng·∫°n's emotions toward H√† Lan in this novel should be seen with empathy even they are not sensible at all. H√† Lan can be observed as a typical beautiful girl who changes her environment from rural to urban. And lastly, Tr√† Long- a cute girl with all the good traits, but turns out to be just a copy or someone else's replacement. It's bitter and it's hard to accept, but again it's realistic.
